      <script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

  P.when("A", "a-dropdown", "HSXErrorModal","ready").execute(function(A, dropdownController, errorModal) {

    var $btnCreateList = A.$("#landing-btn-create-list");

    var $inputGrade = A.$("#landing-select-grade-level");
    var $inputGradeSelector = dropdownController.getSelect("landing-select-grade-level");
    $inputGrade.bind("change", function(event) {
      var grade = $inputGradeSelector.val();
      var url = "";
      if (grade == -2) {
        url = "/b/ref=hsx_sl_ln_gl_oth?_encoding=UTF8&ie=UTF8&node=1069242";
      } else if (grade >= -1 && grade <= 5) {
        url = "/b/ref=hsx_sl_ln_gl_Kt5?_encoding=UTF8&ie=UTF8&node=7133972011";
      } else if (grade >= 6 && grade <= 8) {
        url = "/b/ref=hsx_sl_ln_gl_6t8?_encoding=UTF8&ie=UTF8&node=7133975011";
      } else if (grade >= 9 && grade <= 12) {
        url = "/b/ref=hsx_sl_ln_gl_9t12?_encoding=UTF8&ie=UTF8&node=7133977011";
      }
      window.location.href = url;
    });

    var generateAuthLink = function(successCallback, errorCallback) {
      A.ajax("/gp/school-lists/ajax/ajax-generate-auth-url.html/ref=hsx_sl_ajx_au_ln", {
        method: "POST",
        params: {
          data: "hsx/createList",
          returnURI: "/gp/school-lists/create/ref=hsx_sl_cli_ln",
        },
        success: function(result) {
          if (result.succeeded) {
            if (successCallback) {
              successCallback(result);
            }
          } else {
            if (errorCallback) {
              errorCallback(result);
            }
          }
        },
        error: function(error) {
          if (errorCallback) {
            errorCallback(error);
          }
        }
      });
    }


    var createList = function() {
      A.ajax("/gp/school-lists/ajax/ajax-create-hsxlist.html/ref=hsx_sl_ajx_cl_ln", {
        method: "POST",
        params: {
          listType: "classroom",
          token: "gItIKdjyVu3BF103NrFIfHXVnI8DGmVC1MrqsKwAAAADAAAAAFOQTmxyYXcAAAAA"
        },
        dataType: "json",
        success: function(result) {
          if (result.succeeded == 1) {
            var hasLists = false;
            localStorage.setItem("newVisitor", !hasLists);

            var baseURL = "/gp/school-lists/edit/{{hsxListId}}/ref=hsx_sl_ed_ln?ie=UTF8&newVisitor=1";
            window.location.href = baseURL.replace(/\{\{hsxListId\}\}/, result.hsxListId);
          } else {
            errorModal.show("There was an error while creating your list. Please try again.");
            $btnCreateList.removeClass("a-button-disabled");
          }

        },
        error: function(result) {
          errorModal.show("There was an error while creating your list. Please try again.");
          $btnCreateList.removeClass("a-button-disabled");
        }
      });
    }

    A.declarative("landing-create-list", "click", function(event) {
      if ($btnCreateList.hasClass("a-button-disabled"))
        return;
      $btnCreateList.addClass("a-button-disabled");

      if (event.data.authed == 0) {
        generateAuthLink(function(result) {
          localStorage.setItem("newVisitor", true);
          window.location.href = result.authURL;
        }, function(error) {
          errorModal.show("There was an error while creating your list. Please try again.");
          $btnCreateList.removeClass("a-button-disabled");
        });
      } else {
        createList();
      }
    });
  });

//]]>
      </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[


P.when("A","ready").execute(function schoolResultsDisplayReady(A) {
    var resultsFound     = 0;
    var page             = 1;
    var startIndex       = 0;
    var totalPages       = 10;
    var pageCap          = parseInt("50", 10);
    var resultSize       = parseInt("10", 10);
    var fieldSearchTerms = [];
    var searchText       = A.trim(A.$("#schoolSearchBox").val());
    var searchURL        = "/gp/school-lists/ajax/ajax-search-schools.html/ref=hsx_sl_ajx_ss_ln";
    var ddGenURL         = "/gp/school-lists/ajax/ajax-display-school-lists.html/ref=hsx_sl_ajx_ldd_ln";
    var stringNResults   = "Showing {0} - {1} of {2} Results";
    var stringListsFor   = "{0} lists found for this school";
    var stringOneList    = "1 list found for this school";
    var stringViewLists  = "View lists for {0}";
    var currentSchools   = [];
    var upperBound;
    var filterType       = "zip_code";

    var emptyDropdown    = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-dropdown.hsxss-school-1").html();
    var allDropdowns     = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-dropdown");

    var pageButtons      = A.$(".hsx-ss-page");
    var buttonOutput     = [A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-1"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-2"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-3"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-4"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-5"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-6"),
                              A.$("#hsx-ss-pb-7")];

    var pageDots         = A.$(".hsx-ss-pdot");
    var buttonDotLeft    = A.$("#hsx-ss-pdot-left");
    var buttonDotMid     = A.$("#hsx-ss-pdot-mid");
    var buttonDotRight   = A.$("#hsx-ss-pdot-right");

    var paginationList   = A.$('ul.a-pagination li');
    var pagePrev         = paginationList.first();
    var pageNext         = paginationList.last();

    var searchBox        = A.$("#schoolSearchBox");
    var filterBox        = A.$("#hsx-ss-filtertext");
    var filterDropdown   = A.$("#hsx-school-sortby");
    var showingResults   = A.$("#showingNResults");
    var errorNoResults   = A.$("#hsx-ss-noresults");
    var errorTryAgain    = A.$("#hsx-ss-generalerror");
    var errorRefineMore  = A.$("#hsx-ss-refinefurther");
    var loadIndicator    = A.$("#school-search-loading-indicator");

    var slotCenter4      = A.$("#hsx-ss-center-4-wrapper");
    var slotCenter5      = A.$("#hsx-ss-center-5-wrapper");
    var slotCenter6      = A.$("#hsx-ss-center-6-wrapper");
    var slotCenter7      = A.$("#hsx-ss-center-7-wrapper");
    var slotCenter8      = A.$("#hsx-ss-center-8-wrapper");

    var searchContainer  = A.$("#hsx-list-school-results-display-container");
    var topBar           = A.$("#hsx-ss-topbar");
    var schoolResults    = A.$(".hsx-ss-schoolresults");
    var paginationDiv    = A.$('.hsx-ss-resultspagination');

    var schoolSearchAjax = undefined;

    var searchSchools = function(){
        hideLandingSlots();
        errorTryAgain.addClass('a-hidden');
        errorNoResults.addClass('a-hidden');
        errorRefineMore.addClass('a-hidden');
        loadIndicator.removeClass("a-hidden");
        searchContainer.addClass("a-hidden");

        startIndex = (page-1) * resultSize;

        if(schoolSearchAjax !== undefined)
            schoolSearchAjax.abort();
        schoolSearchAjax = A.ajax(searchURL, {
            method: "POST",
            params: {
                searchQuery: searchText,
                startIndex: startIndex,
                resultSize: resultSize,
                fieldSearchTerms: JSON.stringify(fieldSearchTerms),
                needListCounts: 1,
            },
            success: function(results) {
                schoolSearchAjax = undefined;
                if (!results.error){
                    allDropdowns.hide();
                    currentSchools = results.Schools;
                    resultsFound = parseInt(results.resultsFound, 10);

                    if (!resultsFound) {
                        loadIndicator.addClass("a-hidden");
                        errorNoResults.removeClass('a-hidden');
                        showingResults.hide();
                        schoolResults.addClass("a-hidden");
                        A.$(".a-pagination").hide();
                        searchContainer.removeClass('a-hidden');
                        return;
                    } else {
                        schoolResults.removeClass("a-hidden");
                        errorNoResults.addClass('a-hidden');
                        showingResults.show();
                    }

                    var displayTotal = Math.ceil(resultsFound/resultSize);
                    var resultsDisplay;
                    totalPages = Math.min(displayTotal, pageCap);
                    if (displayTotal > totalPages) {
                        errorRefineMore.removeClass('a-hidden');
                        resultsDisplay = (pageCap * resultSize).toString() + "+";
                    } else {
                        resultsDisplay = resultsFound;
                    }

                    upperBound = startIndex + resultSize;
                    upperBound = ((upperBound <= resultsFound) ? upperBound : resultsFound);
                    var resultsCount = sFormat(stringNResults, (startIndex+1), upperBound, resultsDisplay);
                    showingResults.text(resultsCount);

                    if (totalPages > 1) {
                        A.$(".a-pagination").show();
                    } else {
                        A.$(".a-pagination").hide();
                    }

                    paginate(page, totalPages);
                    paginationDiv.removeClass("a-hidden");

                    for (var schoolRank = 1; schoolRank < 11; schoolRank++) {
                        var schoolCSSClass = '.hsxss-school-' + schoolRank;
                        var schoolRow      = A.$(".hsx-ss-schoolrow" + schoolCSSClass);
                        var schoolDivider  = A.$(".hsx-ss-divider" + schoolCSSClass);
                        var schoolData     = currentSchools[schoolRank-1];
                        if (schoolData) {
                            var showListLink  = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-showlist" + schoolCSSClass);
                            var hideListLink  = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-hidelist" + schoolCSSClass);
                            var listDropdown  = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-dropdown" + schoolCSSClass);
                            var shopBy        = A.$(".hsx-ss-shopby" + schoolCSSClass);
                            var schoolName    = schoolData.name;
                            var schoolAddress = [   schoolData.street + ".",
                                                    schoolData.city + ",",
                                                    schoolData.state,
                                                    schoolData.zipCode
                                                ].join(" ");
                            var schoolId = schoolData.id;
                            var schoolListCount = parseInt(schoolData.listCount,10);

                            A.$(".hsxschoolname"    + schoolCSSClass).text(schoolName);
                            A.$(".hsxschooladdress" + schoolCSSClass).text(schoolAddress);
                            if (schoolListCount > 0){
                                if (schoolListCount === 1){
                                    var listDropdownPrompt = stringOneList;
                                } else {
                                    var listDropdownPrompt = sFormat(stringListsFor, schoolListCount.toString());
                                }
                                A.$(".hsxlistcount" + schoolCSSClass).text(listDropdownPrompt);
                                generateDropdown(schoolId, schoolRank, listDropdown);

                                shopBy.addClass('a-hidden');
                                hideListLink.addClass('a-hidden');
                                showListLink.removeClass('a-hidden');
                                showListLink.text(sFormat(stringViewLists, schoolName));
                            } else {
                                A.$(".hsxlistcount" + schoolCSSClass).text("This school has not submitted any supply lists.");
                                listDropdown.html(emptyDropdown);

                                showListLink.addClass('a-hidden');
                                hideListLink.addClass('a-hidden');
                                shopBy.removeClass('a-hidden');
                            }
                            schoolRow.show();
                            schoolDivider.removeClass('a-hidden');
                        } else {
                            schoolRow.hide();
                            schoolDivider.addClass('a-hidden');
                        }
                    }
                    searchContainer.removeClass('a-hidden');
                } else {
                    errorTryAgain.removeClass('a-hidden');
                }
                loadIndicator.addClass("a-hidden");
            },
            error: function(results) {
                loadIndicator.addClass("a-hidden");
                errorTryAgain.removeClass('a-hidden');
            }
        });
    };

    var topLevelSearch = function(){

        if (searchBox.hasClass("ie-input-placeholder")) {
            return;
        }

        searchText = A.trim(searchBox.val());
        if (searchText.length > 0 && searchText != searchBox.attr("placeholder")) {
        page = 1;
        startIndex = 0;
        fieldSearchTerms = [];
        filterBox.val('');
        searchSchools();
        } else {
            return;
        }
    };

    var filterSearch = function(){
        var filterText = A.trim(filterBox.val());
        if (!filterText) {
            topLevelSearch();
        } else {
            if (searchText.length > 0) {
                searchBox.val(searchText);
                page = 1;
                startIndex = 0;
                fieldSearchTerms = [{name: filterType, value: filterText}];
                searchSchools();
            } else {
                return;
            }
        }
    };

    var toggleListDropdown = function(listDropdown, showListLink, hideListLink){
        showListLink.toggleClass('a-hidden');
        hideListLink.toggleClass('a-hidden');
        A.slideToggle(listDropdown, 200, 'ease-out');
    };

    var generateDropdown = function(schoolId, schoolRank, dropdownSelector){
        A.ajax(ddGenURL, {
            method: "POST",
            params: {
                "schoolId": schoolId,
                "schoolRank": schoolRank,
            },
            success: function(results) {
                dropdownSelector.html(results);
            }
        });
    };

    var sFormat = function (string){
        var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1);
        return string.replace(/{(\d+)}/g, function(hit, count) {
            return typeof args[count] != 'undefined' ? args[count] : hit;
        });
    };

    var paginate = function(currentPage, maxPages){
        if (currentPage > maxPages) { return;}
        if (currentPage < 1) {currentPage = 1;}

        pageDots.hide();
        pageButtons.hide();
        pageButtons.removeClass('a-selected');
        allDropdowns.hide();
        var buttonArray = [1, false, false, false, false, false, false];
        var edgeDistance = Math.min(currentPage-1, maxPages-currentPage);
        var singleRun = false;

        if (maxPages >= 7) {
            buttonArray[6] = maxPages;
            switch (edgeDistance) {
                case 0:
                case 1:
                    if (currentPage === 1 || currentPage === 2) {
                        buttonArray[1] = 2;
                        buttonArray[2] = 3;
                    } else {
                        buttonArray[4] = maxPages-2;
                        buttonArray[5] = maxPages-1;
                    }
                    break;
                case 2:
                    if (currentPage === 3) {
                        buttonArray[1] = 2;
                        buttonArray[2] = 3;
                        buttonArray[3] = 4;
                    } else {
                        buttonArray[3] = maxPages-3;
                        buttonArray[4] = maxPages-2;
                        buttonArray[5] = maxPages-1;
                    }
                    break;
                case 3:
                    if (maxPages === 7 && currentPage === 4) {
                        singleRun = true;
                        break;
                    }
                default:
                    buttonArray[2] = currentPage-1;
                    buttonArray[3] = currentPage;
                    buttonArray[4] = currentPage+1;
                    break;
            }
        } else if (maxPages <= 5) {
            singleRun = true;
        } else if (maxPages ===  6 && (currentPage !== 1 && currentPage !== 6)) {
            singleRun = true;
        }

        if (singleRun) {
            for (var i = maxPages - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                buttonArray[i] = i+1;
            }
        } else {
            if (currentPage >= 5) {
                buttonDotLeft.show();
            }
            if (currentPage <= maxPages-4) {
                buttonDotRight.show();
            }
            if (buttonArray[2] === 3){
                buttonArray[1] = 2;
            }
            if (buttonArray[4] === maxPages-2){
                buttonArray[5] = maxPages-1;
            }
        }

        for (var i = buttonArray.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
            if (buttonArray[i]) {
                buttonOutput[i].children("a").text(buttonArray[i]);
                buttonOutput[i].unbind("click");
                buttonOutput[i].bind("click", function(){
                    page = parseInt(A.$(this).children("a").text(), 10);
                    searchSchools();
                });
                buttonOutput[i].show();
            } else {
                buttonOutput[i].hide();
                buttonOutput[i].unbind("click");
            }
        }

        pageNext.unbind("click");
        pagePrev.unbind("click");

        if (currentPage === 1) {
            disablePageButton(pagePrev);
        }
        if (currentPage === maxPages) {
            disablePageButton(pageNext);
        }
        if (currentPage + 1 <= maxPages) {
            enablePageButton(pageNext);
            pageNext.bind("click", function(){
                page += 1;
                searchSchools();
            });
        }
        if (currentPage - 1 >= 1) {
            enablePageButton(pagePrev);
            pagePrev.bind("click", function(){
                page -= 1;
                searchSchools();
            });
        }

        var activeButton = pageButtons.filter(function() {
            return A.$(this).children("a").text() == currentPage;
        });

        activeButton.addClass('a-selected');
    };

    var enablePageButton = function (pageButton){
        pageButton.removeClass("a-disabled");
        pageButton.children().replaceWith(function(){
            return A.$("<a>" + A.$(this).html() + "</a>");
        });
    }

    var disablePageButton = function (pageButton){
        pageButton.addClass("a-disabled");
        pageButton.children().replaceWith(function(){
            return A.$("<div>" + A.$(this).html() + "</div>");
        });
    }

    var hideLandingSlots = function (){
        slotCenter4.hide();
        slotCenter5.hide();
        slotCenter6.hide();
        slotCenter7.hide();
        slotCenter8.hide();
        return;
    }

    A.declarative('hsx-top-search-box', 'keypress', function(event){
        if (event.$event.keyCode == 13) {
            topLevelSearch();
        }
    });

    A.declarative('hsx-top-search-button', 'click', function(event){
            topLevelSearch();
    });

    A.declarative('hsx-filter-box', 'keypress', function(event){
        if (event.$event.keyCode == 13) {
            filterSearch();
        }
    });

    A.declarative('hsx-filter-button', 'click', function(event){
        filterSearch();
    });

    for (var i = 1; i < 11; i++) {
        (function() {
            var showListLink = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-showlist.hsxss-school-" + i);
            var hideListLink = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-hidelist.hsxss-school-" + i);
            var listDropdown = A.$(".hsx-ss-slist-dropdown.hsxss-school-" + i);
            A.declarative('hsx-togglelist-'+i, 'click', function(event){
                toggleListDropdown(listDropdown, showListLink, hideListLink);
            });
        })();
    };

    A.on("a:dropdown:selected:schoolfilter", function (data) {
      filterType = data.value;
    });

    if (searchText) {
        topLevelSearch();
    }
});

//]]>
        </script>

//<![CDATA[

P.when("A","ready").execute("IEPlaceholderPolyfill", function IEPlaceholderPolyfill(A) {
    if (!A.capabilities.inputPlaceholder) {
        A.$("input[type='text'][placeholder], input[type='search'][placeholder]").each(function initIEInputs(index) {
            var $input = A.$(this);
            if ($input.val() === "") {
                $input.addClass("ie-input-placeholder").val($input.attr("placeholder"));
            }
        });

        A.$("body").delegate("input[type='text'][placeholder], input[type='search'][placeholder]", "focus", function focusIE(event) {
            var $input = A.$(event.target);
            if ($input.hasClass("ie-input-placeholder") && $input.val() === $input.attr("placeholder")) {
                $input.val("");
            }
            $input.removeClass("ie-input-placeholder");
        }).delegate("input[type='text'][placeholder], input[type='search'][placeholder]", "blur", function blurIE(event) {
            var $input = A.$(event.target);
            if ($input.val() === "") {
                $input.val($input.attr("placeholder"));
                $input.addClass("ie-input-placeholder");
            }
        });

    }
});

//]]>
        </script>
